NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

N. Arumugam, a male child born to M. Natarajan on 20-05-1988, residing at 59, Odaikarai Thoppu, Krishnaperi,
(Gandhinagar Post), Tirunelveli Town-627 008 has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
at Siva Vishnu Hospital, Bangaluru. The same has been medically examined by Dr. K. Neelathatchi, B.Sc.,M.B.B.S.,
Medical Officer, Govt. Primary Health Centre, Ukkirankottai, Tirunelveli. By this I, may be treated as a female and shall
henceforth be known as N. ASIN.
Tirunelveli,
8th September 2015.

N. ARUMUGAM.

Notice is hereby given that, pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, the Company in terms of Section
484(1) of the Companies Act, 1956 a Special Resolution was passed at the Annual General Meeting and Meeting of the
Creditors’ held on 17-08-2015 at 11.00 AM and 12.00 PM respectively, to wind up the Company by Creditors’ Voluntary
Winding Up.
In pursuant to the resolution passed, the Company and the Creditors’ have appointed Mr. Saji P John, Advocate,
SPJ Legal, Advocates, Bangalore as Liquidator of the Company for the purpose of such winding up as per the provisions
of the Companies Act, 1956.
for Motonic India Automotive Pvt., Ltd.

Notice is hereby given that the Members of AVTS2 Virtual Lifestyle Private Limited at their Extra-ordinary General Meeting
held on Tuesday, the 01st September, 2015 at 11.00 A.M. at No. 60, Rukmani Lakshmipathi Salai,
Egmore, Chennai-600 008 have passed the following Special Resolutions to wind up the above company voluntarily.

1.

Members Voluntary Winding up

“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the consent of the
Members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as the “Members
Voluntary Winding up”, with effect from 31st March, 2015.”
2.

Appointment of Liquidator

“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provision of Section 490 of the Companies Act, 1956, consent of the Members
of the Company be and is hereby accorded to appoint Mr. V. Suresh, Practising Company Secretary, (Regn. No. C.P. 6032)
#28, Ganapathy Colony, 3rd Street, Teynampet, Chennai-600 018, as Liquidator of the Company at a remuneration
of Rs. 1,00,000/- (Rupees One Lakh Only) excluding the payment of Service Tax and reimbursement of out of
pocket expenses.”
Chennai,
11th September 2015.

K. SURESH,
